    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer4408991521466985413">Book One: Sporadic Memories is a novel about a lifestyle that needs to be read about. Within the first few pages you will realize there has been a loss, it is not sad though; the narrator expresses with great enthusiasm the life they lived, which makes it nice during the times when it becomes difficult to read. <br/>By the first few pages I hope you can hear the narrator has be</span>
  <span id="freeText4408991521466985413" style="display:none">Book One: Sporadic Memories is a novel about a lifestyle that needs to be read about. Within the first few pages you will realize there has been a loss, it is not sad though; the narrator expresses with great enthusiasm the life they lived, which makes it nice during the times when it becomes difficult to read. <br />By the first few pages I hope you can hear the narrator has been alive for a long time, explaining the way it is written? <br />There is no distinction between the characters’ genders, which offers a personal experience for the reader. <br />The part that remembers the time they gave bracelets to each other brings about another way of joining together in marriage … following how their courtship developed, and the apple tree that is depicted throughout the novel using its fruit in traditional family recipes. It gets sad for a bit after this, but notice that it gets sad because there is so much more to why the one lost is worth writing about. <br />It is partly a love story. You know for sure it is when you get to the parts about the piano played and songs written … you should at first read to the first song. The memory at the exhibition and recalling times in the rain and snow are next. They traveled a lot together and you will read of a place if you read a little past the description of the surroundings of their home. <br />If you read to the first birthday mentioned; you will find a recipe worth trying, a poem worth reading, and fireworks. The narrator is a playwright, so there is a play that is broken down throughout the novel … it is a difficult read, but it is important in showing how the two brought their work together, and what positive influences they made upon those they met.<br />Things are repeated to show how important positive repetition is, which helps to move past pain while remembering the passion. This novel is full of passion, carried throughout the life they had for each other, their work, and their friends … you might want to read through first until you hear about their friends. <br />This novel completes the story as the pages turn; putting certain pages together will bring the memories in order. <br />It is an easy read. <br />It is written poetically, which gives it justice. It begins the way it ends … <br />Book One: Sporadic Memories is a novel about a lifestyle that needs to be read about.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13230091-angel-gelique?shelf=brilliant">brilliant</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13230091-angel-gelique?shelf=creative-and-imaginative">creative-and-imaginative</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2671194183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6854531822241889206"><i>
  <b>“Merry of Your Start”</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>“The sky is now a vibrant red as I mark against the dawn; it has been a while since the color of the sky was like this. I remember a time when I was inspiring with you: a now sporadic memory flowing through my mind.”</i><br/><br/>First, I have to say that this book is chock full of all things awesome! It’s not just a story, it’s a little bit of everything, including beautiful illustrations and some amazing recipes. There are plenty of great surprises. I’ve never come across anything l</span>
  <span id="freeText6854531822241889206" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“Merry of Your Start”</b>
</i><br /><br /><i>“The sky is now a vibrant red as I mark against the dawn; it has been a while since the color of the sky was like this. I remember a time when I was inspiring with you: a now sporadic memory flowing through my mind.”</i><br /><br />First, I have to say that this book is chock full of all things awesome! It’s not just a story, it’s a little bit of everything, including beautiful illustrations and some amazing recipes. There are plenty of great surprises. I’ve never come across anything like it before and I’m truly impressed by Ms. Marsman’s creativity and brilliance!<br /><br />A good portion of this book is about love and loss, yet it is not sad and depressing. Rather, love is celebrated in such a way that even though the loved one is gone, they are still present in such incredibly profound ways. It’s as though memory itself gets solidified into reality, cheating death and restoring all it prematurely stripped away.<br /><br /><i>“It is all these little things we did over and over that keep me alive....”</i><br /><br />The words are deep, profound and hauntingly beautiful. Rememberance yields a sort of magic. Through loving memories, the narrator keeps her beloved alive; she brings her dear one back to her life.<br /><br />But it’s not only love in the romantic sense that’s discussed in this book; there’s the strong bonds of familial love, too. Traditions are kept alive and passed down to new generations. <br /><br />There’s also the empowerment of women everywhere through heightened self-esteem and confidence. <br /><br />This is a highly motivational book that will leave readers feeling positive and inspired. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6854531822241889206" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5028934235955161836">This book is written in a very lyrical style which comes across as haunting poetry.<br/>The female narrator tells us of her great love, a union of mind and soul, and then of the loss of that love.   <span id="freeText5028934235955161836" style="display:none">This book is written in a very lyrical style which comes across as haunting poetry.<br />The female narrator tells us of her great love, a union of mind and soul, and then of the loss of that love. This author weaves a lovely spell and draws you in to the almost musical tone of the story. She has published several other books: some contain visual images and recipes (which I always enjoy seeing).The author is also a Canadian, and I am so happy and proud to support another Canadian author.<br />Keep up the great work, Ali Marsman: we should all be as free and unafraid of expressing our deepest emotions as you obviously are.</span>

<div id="review_2657145151" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2657145151" />
    <a title="Eugenie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24455451-eugenie"><img alt="Eugenie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1382760775p2/24455451.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2657145151?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eugenie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eugenie" href="/user/show/24455451-eugenie">Eugenie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2657145151" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3566797342166887738">Author Ali Marsman has created a masterpiece of human emotions. As I read her "Sporadic Memories", I was touched on a profound level by the main character’s endearing account of life, love and loss. <br/><br/>There is no abject despondency or deep depression conveyed, however, but barely a tinge of sadness – just enough to add drama to the narration. <br/><br/>The stronger emotion that dominated my psyche as I read was one of hope, since the character seems to draw strength from her memories. Her “Sporadic Memories</span>
  <span id="freeText3566797342166887738" style="display:none">Author Ali Marsman has created a masterpiece of human emotions. As I read her "Sporadic Memories", I was touched on a profound level by the main character’s endearing account of life, love and loss. <br /><br />There is no abject despondency or deep depression conveyed, however, but barely a tinge of sadness – just enough to add drama to the narration. <br /><br />The stronger emotion that dominated my psyche as I read was one of hope, since the character seems to draw strength from her memories. Her “Sporadic Memories” keep her loved one alive and makes her strong. <br /><br />Although she lives on without her lifetime companion, yet he remains with her every minute of every day. I felt his presence as she shared their routines. He was there in the celebrations of birthdays and anniversaries, he was there as she met with friends on occasions, he was alive in the music, he was there as she shared the recipes that they created together. And she still encountered him beneath the apple tree which they planted together. Like the apple tree, he remains alive to her.<br /><br />This is a thought -provoking work – it will be a good companion for someone facing the loss of a dear loved one. <br /><br />I’m glad that I purchased the paperback copy as the illustrations are simply exquisite.<br /><br />It’s 5 wonderful stars from me and I will certainly be re-visiting “Sporadic Memories” from time to time in the future.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3566797342166887738" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/64693656?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erma Odrach" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erma Odrach" href="/user/show/1339678-erma-odrach">Erma Odrach</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer64693656" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7860540855783871677">This is not a novel in the normal sense of the word but a novel of poetry; it is about love and loss and about time and life. The apple on the cover symbolizes ecstasy, fertility, abundance and love, and when an apple tree is planted on pg. 160, it brings with it inspiration. I love the recipes that follow: apple pie, curried apple soup, apple butter and more. I even tried a couple (apple baked pancakes and apple jelly) and both were really good. Honest and engaging, this is a book from the hear</span>
  <span id="freeText7860540855783871677" style="display:none">This is not a novel in the normal sense of the word but a novel of poetry; it is about love and loss and about time and life. The apple on the cover symbolizes ecstasy, fertility, abundance and love, and when an apple tree is planted on pg. 160, it brings with it inspiration. I love the recipes that follow: apple pie, curried apple soup, apple butter and more. I even tried a couple (apple baked pancakes and apple jelly) and both were really good. Honest and engaging, this is a book from the heart.</span>

<div id="review_69781653" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/69781653" />
    <a title="Urenna Sander" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2430778-urenna-sander"><img alt="Urenna Sander" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442500675p2/2430778.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/69781653?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Urenna Sander" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Urenna Sander" href="/user/show/2430778-urenna-sander">Urenna Sander</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781897512111" href="/book/show/3830244-sporadic-memories">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer69781653" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6269550771507842979">Throughout the book, Ali Marsman’s writing invoked almost continuous, intense love and yearning. The person, who I presume passed, was much loved and revered. Some passages are beautifully written and heartfelt. The theme appeared to be apples, which is depicted on her book cover. <br/><br/>Apples have many symbolisms, but I think the symbols in Ali’s book are love, beauty, and remembrance. The apple tree represents immortality; the person will always be alive in their heart. There are several apple recip</span>
  <span id="freeText6269550771507842979" style="display:none">Throughout the book, Ali Marsman’s writing invoked almost continuous, intense love and yearning. The person, who I presume passed, was much loved and revered. Some passages are beautifully written and heartfelt. The theme appeared to be apples, which is depicted on her book cover. <br /><br />Apples have many symbolisms, but I think the symbols in Ali’s book are love, beauty, and remembrance. The apple tree represents immortality; the person will always be alive in their heart. There are several apple recipes in the book.<br /><br />Ali is a playwright; snippets of a play were interwoven throughout the book. This should have been omitted. Other than that, I enjoyed Sporadic Memories.<br /><br />Although considered a novel, I think this is a book of poetry. <br /><br />I completed Book One of Sporadic Memories in 2019. The book concerns the eternal love, at times written poetically between an artist (writer) and pianist (musician). The musician passes away and the writer's world changes. She yearns for his source of comfort, unconditional love, and physical intimacy. Special days are remembered; here she talks with wonder about their love and, surprisingly, it is not a minefield of grief, but only her everlasting love, even as she ages. I thought there should be a time to mourn, yet go on living. But there are no rules about how you should feel, nor right or wrong way to mourn. Apples, mentioned through out the book are symbolic of immortality.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6269550771507842979" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NPQjYe+sDT6unPI3m124W+ERCIBJuxTNBQKvFXiAhAkg15EhHQUyvb1+ldQNMU7wtooG/f057uSN3I5i3bokBw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YMeFAWzb7I5FE1mmqYQz6JMjSQ3hMA8JCQrAJf9Sh8105DdBnnLTDVbxPkU/6MVDxLhHcFWy9SCB1OFSWmgnww==')})
  }

His logical, methodical world was suddenly turned upside down by a strangely exotic woman living on a tropical island thousands of miles away. Who is Sabine? How can she &quot;see&quot; what Griffin is painting when they have never met? Is she a long-lost twin? A clairvoyant? Or a malevolent angel? Are we witnessing the flowering of a magical relationship or a descent into madness?\n\nThis stunning visual novel unfolds in a series of postcards and letters, all brilliantly illustrated with whimsical designs, bizarre creatures, and darkly imagined landscapes. Inside the book, Griffin and Sabine\'s letters are to be found nestling in their envelopes, permitting the reader to examine the intimate correspondence of these inexplicably linked strangers. This truly innovative novel combines a strangely fascinating story with lush artwork in an altogether original format.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"8567355332250862132\" href=\"#\" Be legible. Be creative.\n\nIt all began with an idea Frank Warren had for a community art project. He began handing out postcards to strangers and leaving them in public places -- asking people to write down a secret they had never told anyone and mail it to him, anonymously.\n\nThe response was overwhelming. The secrets were both provocative and profound, and the cards themselves were works of art -- carefully and creatively constructed by hand. Addictively compelling, the cards reveal our deepest fears, desires, regrets, and obsessions. Frank calls them &quot;graphic haiku,&quot; beautiful, elegant, and small in structure but powerfully emotional.\n\nAs Frank began posting the cards on his website, PostSecret took on a life of its own, becoming much more than a simple art project. It has grown into a global phenomenon, exposing our individual aspirations, fantasies, and frailties -- our common humanity.\n\nEvery day dozens of postcards still make their way to Frank, with postmarks from around the world, touching on every aspect of human experience. This extraordinary collection brings together the most powerful, personal, and beautifully intimate secrets Frank Warren has received -- and brilliantly illuminates that human emotions can be unique <span id="freeTextContainer11977627799353779850">Ali Marsman was born in Nova Scotia in 1978; she spent twenty-five years living there, and now lives in British Columbia. Her first books, 'Heal With Me' and 'Our Journey Goes On' sent her on a journey throughout Canada presenting motivational workshops and speeches, in schools, group homes, shelters, and within various other organizations and societies. <br/><br/>Ali has received many awards for her writin</span>
  <span id="freeText11977627799353779850" style="display:none">Ali Marsman was born in Nova Scotia in 1978; she spent twenty-five years living there, and now lives in British Columbia. Her first books, 'Heal With Me' and 'Our Journey Goes On' sent her on a journey throughout Canada presenting motivational workshops and speeches, in schools, group homes, shelters, and within various other organizations and societies. <br /><br />Ali has received many awards for her writing, and has been profiled in magazines, on television programs, and as well as radio. <br /><br />She is also the author of, Book One: Sporadic Memories, Book Two: Because of Grandfather, and Book Too: Because of Grandmother. A trio of books celebrating life with family and friends!</span>
